<i><small> &lt; section | section | jie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;节，小节；部分</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chaptam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; chapter | chapitre | zhang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;章，章节</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pajie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; page | page | ye &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;页，书页</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>papi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; paper | papier | zhi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;纸；文章，论文</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>buku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; book | - | shu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;书，书籍</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vordibuku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;词典；字典</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>filun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; file | fichier | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;文件，档案</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dokun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; document | document | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;文档，档案</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mesajin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; message | message | xin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;信息，消息，口信；报文</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>teksen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; text | texte | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;课<u>文</u>；文本；短文；短信</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>teksenbuku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;课本，教材</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>esen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; essay | essai | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;作<u>文</u>；文章；散文</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lesen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; lesson | leçon | cheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;课<u>程</u>，第...课；一堂课；教训</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>korsen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; course | cours | cheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;课<u>程</u>，系列课</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lektiam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; lecture | - | jiang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;讲座，授课，演讲</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>subju</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; subject | sujet | zhu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;主题；科目，学科</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>noti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; note | note | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;笔记，注释，备注<br> ▹ <b>notiz</b> &nbsp; 做笔记；注意到</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>skoren</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; score | score | fen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;分数</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>marku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; mark | marque | fu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;符号，记号；标志；分数</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gradie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; grade | grade | bie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;级<u>别</u>，等级；年级</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>levie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; level | niveau | bie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;级<u>别</u>，水平</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klasie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; class | classe | bie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;类<u>别</u>；班，班级</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klasietam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;教室；课堂</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sainceu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; science | science | ke &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;科学；自然科学<br> ▹ <b>sainceuje</b> &nbsp; 科学的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tekni</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; technic | technique | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;技术；技法<br> ▹ <b>teknije</b> &nbsp; 技术的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nombu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; number | nombre | shu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;数量，数<br> ▹ <b>nombuje</b> &nbsp; 大量的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fisiku</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; physics | physique | wu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;物理，自然规律<br> ▹ <b>fisikuje</b> &nbsp; 物理的，物质的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kemua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; chemistry | chimie | hua &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;化合，炼金术；合成物，化学品<br> ▹ <b>kemuaz</b> &nbsp; 化合；炼金<br> ▹ <b>kemuaje</b> &nbsp; 化学的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mediki</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; medico- | médicale | yi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;医，医疗；医药<br> ▹ <b>medikiz</b> &nbsp; 医治，治疗<br> ▹ <b>medikije</b> &nbsp; 医疗的，医学的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mediciau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; medicine | médecine | yao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;药，药物，药品<br> ▹ <b>mediciauz</b> &nbsp; 制药；熬药</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>letikso</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;文学<br> ▹ <b>letiksoje</b> &nbsp; 文学的；文绉绉的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lingu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; lingual | lingual | yu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;语言，...语，...话</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>interlingu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;国际语</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nuven</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; news | nouvelles | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;新<u>闻</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stori</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; story | histoire | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;故<u>事</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>novo</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; novel | novela [es] | shuo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;小<u>说</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>movin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; movie | - | ying &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;电<u>影</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>poetri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; poetry | poésie | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;诗，诗歌<br> ▹ <b>poetrije</b> &nbsp; 有诗意的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>arti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; art | art | yi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;艺术，美术<br> ▹ <b>artije</b> &nbsp; 艺术的；文艺的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dramu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; drama | dramu | ju &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;剧，戏剧，歌剧，舞剧</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>musue</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; music | musique | yue &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;乐，音乐</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>instrumi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; instrument | instrument | qi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;乐<u>器</u>；仪器</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pianin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; piano | piano | qin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;钢<u>琴</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>violin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; violin | violon | qin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;提<u>琴</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gita</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; guitar | guitare | ta(jita) &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;吉<u>他</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sporti</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sport | sport | ti &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;体育，运动</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gami</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; game | - | xi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;游<u>戏</u>，嬉戏</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; ball | balle | qiu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;球</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>konfu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; kung-fu | kung-fu | gongfu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;功夫</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>archon</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; arch | archet | gong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;弓</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>arian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; arrow | - | jian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;箭</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dartiau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; darts | - | biao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;镖，飞镖</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tentam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; tent | tente | zhang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;帐篷</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cartu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; chart | carte | tu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;地<u>图</u></p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kompan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; compass | compas | pan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;罗<u>盘</u>，指南针</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chesi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; chess | échecs | qi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;棋</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dicou</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; dice | dés | tou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;骰子</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>militun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; military | millitaire | jun &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;军事，军用；军队<br> ▹ <b>militunje</b> &nbsp; 军事的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>armun</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; army | armée | jun &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;军队；陆军</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>armu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; arm | arme | wu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;武器，装备；武装；武力<br> ▹ <b>armuz</b> &nbsp; 武装，装备</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>geran</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | guerre | zhan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;战争<br> ▹ <b>geranz</b> &nbsp; 宣战</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>batan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; battle | bataille | zhan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;战斗，战争<br> ▹ <b>batanz</b> &nbsp; 战斗；斗争</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tankeu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; tank | tank | ke(tanke) &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;坦克；储罐，油箱，水箱</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; gun | - | qiang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;枪；手枪</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; cannon | cannon | pao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;炮，加农炮</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bulan</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; bullet | balle | dan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;弹，子弹，炮弹</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>histori</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; history | histoire | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;历史<br> ▹ <b>historiz</b> &nbsp; 使成为历史，留名青史<br> ▹ <b>historije</b> &nbsp; 历史的，历史性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>politen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; politics | politique | zheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;政治<br> ▹ <b>politenz</b> &nbsp; 政治化<br> ▹ <b>politenje</b> &nbsp; 政治的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>filoseu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; philosophy | philosophie | zhe &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;哲理；道理<br> ▹ <b>filoseuje</b> &nbsp; 哲学的；有哲理的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lua</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; law | loi | fa &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;法律<br> ▹ <b>luaz</b> &nbsp; 成为法律，法律化<br> ▹ <b>luaje</b> &nbsp; 法律的；合法的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ekonomin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; economy | économie | jin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;经济<br> ▹ <b>ekonominje</b> &nbsp; 经济的；节俭的，有效率的</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
#### 一般概念
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>chosu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | chose | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;物，事物，东西，存在；事情</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>objektu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; object | objet | wu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;物体；客体，目标；宾语<br> ▹ <b>objektuje</b> &nbsp; 客观的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>solidu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; solid | solide | gu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;固体，固态<br> ▹ <b>soliduz</b> &nbsp; 固化，凝固；使结实，使牢固<br> ▹ <b>soliduje</b> &nbsp; 固态的，稳固的，稳定的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>likuidie</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; liquid | liquide | ye &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;液体，液态<br> ▹ <b>likuidiez</b> &nbsp; 液化，凝结；使液化，使凝结<br> ▹ <b>likuidieje</b> &nbsp; 液态的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gasi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; gas | gaz | qi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;气体，气态<br> ▹ <b>gasiz</b> &nbsp; 气化，蒸发；使气化，使蒸发<br> ▹ <b>gasije</b> &nbsp; 气态的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>forci</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; force | force | li &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;力，力量；武力，军队<br> ▹ <b>forciz</b> &nbsp; 迫使<br> ▹ <b>forcije</b> &nbsp; 有力的，强有力的；有说服力的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pauri</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; power | pouvoir | li &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;力量，能力；功率；电力；权力<br> ▹ <b>paurije</b> &nbsp; 有力量的；有权势的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>enerjen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; energy | énergie | neng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;能量，能源<br> ▹ <b>enerjenje</b> &nbsp; 精力旺盛的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>velocitu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; velocity | vitesse | su &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;速度</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sonen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sonal | son | sheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;声音，声响</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>voicen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; voice | voix | sheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;声音，嗓音（说话或唱歌）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>noisen</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; noise | - | sheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;噪<u>声</u>，噪音</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>toniau</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; tone | ton | yin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;音<u>调</u>；音色；色调</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hiteu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; heat | - | re &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;热，热能，热量<br> ▹ <b>hiteuz</b> &nbsp; 加热<br> ▹ <b>hiteuje</b> &nbsp; 热情的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luam</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; luminary | lumière | guang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;光，光源；灯；光明<br> ▹ <b>luamz</b> &nbsp; 发光；点亮，点燃，点火<br> ▹ <b>luamje</b> &nbsp; 光明的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shadin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; shadow | - | ying &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;影，影子<br> ▹ <b>shadinz</b> &nbsp; 开玩笑<br> ▹ <b>jokiauje</b> &nbsp; 好笑的，滑稽的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>metoda</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; method | méthode | fa &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;方<u>法</u>，办法，手段</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>artifi</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; artifice | artifice | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;诡<u>计</u>，计谋；技巧<br> ▹ <b>artifije</b> &nbsp; 假的，人造的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kustu</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; custom | coutume | su &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;风<u>俗</u>，民俗；习惯</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>riskian</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; risk | risque | xian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;风<u>险</u>，危险<br> ▹ <b>riskianje</b> &nbsp; 危险的，有风险的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>environmin</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; environment | - | jing &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;环<u>境</u>；处境，外界，周围</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
## 基本动词
#### 高频常用
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; is | es | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;是（性质状态）；在（位置）；被（表示被动）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>haz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; has | avoir | - &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;有，拥有；具有<br> ▹ <b>hazo</b> &nbsp; 拥有；拥有的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>doz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; do | - | zuo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;做，施行</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fuez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; feel | - | jue &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;觉，觉得，感觉（系动词）<br> ▹ <b>fuezo</b> &nbsp; 感觉，直感</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>getenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; get | - | cheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;成，变成，成为（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>siamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; seem | sembler | xiang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;像，像是，好像（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>triz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; try | tratar [es] | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;试，尝试；考验；审判<br> ▹ <b>trizo</b> &nbsp; 试验，尝试；审讯</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; want | vouloir | yao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;要，想要<br> ▹ <b>vauzo</b> &nbsp; 愿望</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>doneiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; donate | donner | gei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;给，给予，送给；赠予<br> ▹ <b>doneizo</b> &nbsp; 赠送；赠品；礼品</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>takaz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; take | - | na &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;拿，拿走，取走；带去；服用<br> ▹ <b>takazo</b> &nbsp; 收入，收获</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aluz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | aller | qu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;去，过去</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>venaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | venir | lai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;来，过来</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
#### 基本动作
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; listen | écouter | ting &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;听，倾听（不涉及结果）<br> ▹ <b>tinzo</b> &nbsp; 听，倾听；所闻</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>soz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; say | - | shuo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;说，说话，说道<br> ▹ <b>sozo</b> &nbsp; 说话；所说；言语；说法</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>duz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; read | - | du &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;读，阅读，看书<br> ▹ <b>duzo</b> &nbsp; 阅读</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>riez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; write | écrire | xie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;写，写字，写作<br> ▹ <b>riezo</b> &nbsp; 写作；作品</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; look | - | kan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;看，观看（不涉及结果）<br> ▹ <b>kanzo</b> &nbsp; 看；照看；所见；面容</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smunz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; smell | sentir | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;闻，嗅闻（不涉及结果）<br> ▹ <b>smunzo</b> &nbsp; 气味<br> ▹ <b>smunze</b> &nbsp; 有味道的，臭的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tuchoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; touch | toucher | mo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;摸，触摸（不涉及结果）<br> ▹ <b>tuchozo</b> &nbsp; 触摸；触感</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tastamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; taste | - | chang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;尝，品尝（不涉及结果）<br> ▹ <b>tastamzo</b> &nbsp; 品尝；口味，品味<br> ▹ <b>tastamze</b> &nbsp; 有品位的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;听到，听见（有结果）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;看到，看见（有结果）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tuchauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;摸到（有结果）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smunauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;闻到（有结果）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tastamauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;尝到（有结果）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;听起来（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kanaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;看起来（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tuchaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;摸起来（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smunaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;闻起来（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tastamaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;尝起来，吃起来（系动词）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; run | courir | pao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;跑，跑步<br> ▹ <b>rauzo</b> &nbsp; 跑步，跑步运动；奔跑</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tiauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | sauter | tiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;跳，跳高<br> ▹ <b>tiauzo</b> &nbsp; 跳跃</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fleiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; fly | - | fei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;飞，飞翔<br> ▹ <b>fleizo</b> &nbsp; 飞翔</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>najouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | nager | you &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;游，游泳<br> ▹ <b>najouzo</b> &nbsp; 游泳</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sitoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sit | - | zuo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;坐；坐落</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; stand | - | zhan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;站，站立<br> ▹ <b>stanzo</b> &nbsp; 站立；停留；站台</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; crawl | crawl | pa &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;爬，爬行<br> ▹ <b>krazo</b> &nbsp; 爬行</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>marchouz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; march | marcher | zou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;走，走路；散步<br> ▹ <b>marchouzo</b> &nbsp; 走路，散步</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cruz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; cry | - | ku &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;哭，哭泣，大哭；哭闹<br> ▹ <b>cruzo</b> &nbsp; 哭泣，哭闹</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sobiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sob | sanglotter | ku &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;哭，哭泣，抽泣，啜泣<br> ▹ <b>sobizo</b> &nbsp; 哭泣，抽泣</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lafiauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; laugh | - | xiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;笑，大笑，笑话<br> ▹ <b>lafiauzo</b> &nbsp; 笑声</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smiauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; smile | sourir | xiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;笑，微笑<br> ▹ <b>smiauzo</b> &nbsp; 笑容</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>graz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; grab | - | zhua &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;抓，抓住；理解，领会<br> ▹ <b>grazo</b> &nbsp; 理解</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>putamz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; put | poser | fang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;放，放置</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pushuiz</b>&nbsp; 下落；坠物</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>skraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; scratch | égratigner | zhua &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;抓，抓伤；挠痒<br> ▹ <b>skrazo</b> &nbsp; 抓伤；抓痕</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kikiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; kick | - | ti &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;踢，踹</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hitaz</b>&nbsp; kill | - | sha &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;杀，杀害<br> ▹ <b>kilazo</b> &nbsp; 杀人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pikiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; pick | - | shi &gt; 得到；所得</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fechuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; fetch | chercher | qu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;取，取回，取得</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jetenz</b>&nbsp; #### 生活社交

#### 学习工作
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>edukiauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; educate | éduquer | jiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;教，教育<br> ▹ <b>edukiauzo</b> &nbsp; 教育</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tichauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; teach | - | jiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;教，教书，教学<br> ▹ <b>tichauzo</b> &nbsp; 教学</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>studuez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; study | étudier | xue &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;学，学习，上学，念书；研究<br> ▹ <b>studuezo</b> &nbsp; 学习；研究</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lernuez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; learn | - | xue &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;学，获得信息<br> ▹ <b>lernuezo</b> &nbsp; 学习，模仿</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spelinz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; spell | épeler | pin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;拼写<br> ▹ <b>spelinzo</b> &nbsp; 拼写</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>receiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; recite | réciter | bei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;背诵，复述<br> ▹ <b>receizo</b> &nbsp; 背诵</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kontuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; count | compter | shu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;数，计数<br> ▹ <b>kontuzo</b> &nbsp; 计数</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kalkanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; calculate | calculer | suan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;算，计算，演算，验算<br> ▹ <b>kalkanzo</b> &nbsp; 计算</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kompanz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; add | ajouter | jia &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;加；添加，加入（成分）<br> ▹ <b>adiazo</b> &nbsp; 加法</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>subtrianz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; #### 认知感受

#### 冲突变化
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>conflonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; conflict | - | chong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;冲突；冲撞，抵触<br> ▹ <b>conflonzo</b> &nbsp; 冲突<br> ▹ <b>conflonze</b> &nbsp; 毁灭<br> ▹ <b>destrize</b> &nbsp; 毁灭性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>krakiez</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; crack | craquer | lie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;裂开，破裂，碎裂；使破裂<br> ▹ <b>krakiezo</b> &nbsp; 有威胁的，危险的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>persekoz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; persecute | persécuter | po &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;迫害；压迫<br> ▹ <b>persekozo</b> &nbsp; #### 一般行为
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ekzaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; exist | éxister | zai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;在，存在<br> ▹ <b>ekzaizo</b> &nbsp; 存在；世间万物<br> ▹ <b>ekzaize</b> &nbsp; 存在的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kompiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; compare | comparer | bi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;比，比较<br> ▹ <b>kompizo</b> &nbsp; 对比物；对比结果<br> ▹ <b>kompize</b> &nbsp; 对比的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>apartuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; appertain | appartenir | shu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;属于</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>posesonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; possess | posséder | yong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;拥有，持有，占有<br> ▹ <b>posesonzo</b> &nbsp; 拥有；拥有物</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>uzonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; use | employer | yong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;用，使用<br> ▹ <b>uzonzo</b> &nbsp; 使用，用处；用法<br> ▹ <b>uzonze</b> &nbsp; 有用的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aplonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; apply | appliquer | yong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;用，应用，适用；涂敷（药物）<br> ▹ <b>aplonzo</b> &nbsp; 应用</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aplenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; apply | - | shen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;申请<br> ▹ <b>aplenzo</b> &nbsp; 申请；申请书</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>definz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; 展览</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>montrianz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; demonstrate | montrer | xian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;显示，展示<br> ▹ <b>montrianzo</b> &nbsp; 显示，展示</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>brilauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; brilliant | briller | zhao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;照耀，照亮<br> ▹ <b>brilauzo</b> &nbsp; 照耀；光辉<br> ▹ <b>brilauze</b> &nbsp; 明亮的；光辉的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pleuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; ply | plier | zhe &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;折叠<br> ▹ <b>pleuzo</b> &nbsp; 折叠</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>provenz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; prove | prouver | zheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;证明<br> ▹ <b>provenzo</b> &nbsp; 证明；证据</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dezerviz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; deserve | mériter | zhi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;值得<br> ▹ <b>dezervize</b> &nbsp; 值得的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>indikiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; indicate | indiquer | zhi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;指示<br> ▹ <b>indikizo</b> &nbsp; 指示，指令</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>repitonz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; repeat | répéter | chong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;重复<br> ▹ <b>repitonzo</b> &nbsp; 重复<br> ▹ <b>repitonze</b> &nbsp; 重复性的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dekoranz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; decorate | décorer | zhuang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;装饰<br> ▹ <b>dekoranzo</b> &nbsp; 装饰</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prepeiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; prepare | préparer | bei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;准<u>备</u><br> ▹ <b>prepeizo</b> &nbsp; 准备；准备工作<br> ▹ <b>prepeize</b> &nbsp; 有准备的，准备好了的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>espraz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; express | - | da &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;表<u>达</u>，陈述，表示<br> ▹ <b>esprazo</b> &nbsp; 表达，用语，语句</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kontaktuz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; contact | contacter | chu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;接<u>触</u>；联系<br> ▹ <b>kontaktuzo</b> &nbsp; 接触；联系；联系人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>orijinaiz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; originate |  | lai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;来源于，起源<br> ▹ <b>orijinaizo</b> &nbsp; 来源，起源；起点，原点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>repauz</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; report | rapporter | bao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;报告；报道<br> ▹ <b>repauzo</b> &nbsp; 报告，报道</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
## 基本形容词
#### 外观状态
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bone</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; bona | bonne | bang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;好，好的，棒的<br> ▹ <b>boneo</b> &nbsp; 好事；好人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mave</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; mad | mauvaise | cha &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;坏，坏的，差的<br> ▹ <b>maveo</b> &nbsp; 坏事；坏人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>beile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; belle | belle | mei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;美，美丽，漂亮<br> ▹ <b>beileo</b> &nbsp; 美丽；美丽的东西；美人<br> ▹ <b>beilez</b> &nbsp; 美化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ougle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; ugle | - | chou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;丑，丑的，丑陋<br> ▹ <b>ougleo</b> &nbsp; 丑陋；丑陋的东西；丑鬼<br> ▹ <b>ouglez</b> &nbsp; 丑化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lamge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; long | long | chang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;长，长的，高的（人）<br> ▹ <b>lamgeo</b> &nbsp; 长度<br> ▹ <b>lamgez</b> &nbsp; 加长</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; short | - | duan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;短，短的，矮的（人）<br> ▹ <b>shantez</b> &nbsp; 缩短</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>haute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; high | haute | gao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;高，高的（位置）<br> ▹ <b>hauteo</b> &nbsp; 高度<br> ▹ <b>hautez</b> &nbsp; 增高</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>baise</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; base | basse | ai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;矮，低的（位置）<br> ▹ <b>baisez</b> &nbsp; 压低，降低</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vande</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; wide | - | kuan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;宽，宽的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>naire</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; narrow | - | zhai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;窄，窄的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gronde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; grand | grand | hong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;宏，宏大，宏伟，伟大，盛大<br> ▹ <b>grondeo</b> &nbsp; 伟大；壮举，伟绩；伟人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; giant | - | ju &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;巨，巨大的，极大的<br> ▹ <b>juteo</b> &nbsp; 巨人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>larje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; large | large | da &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;大，大的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>monde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; medium | milieu | zhong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;中，中等的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smiaule</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; small | - | xiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;小，小的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tine</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; tiny | petit | xi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;细，细小的，微小的，袖珍的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>numore</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; numerous | numeroso [es] | duo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;多，很多的，许多的；大量的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>moche</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; much | mucho [es] | duo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;多，多的<br> ▹ <b>mocheo</b> &nbsp; 大量</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>laute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; little | - | shao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;少，少的<br> ▹ <b>lauteo</b> &nbsp; 少量，少许，一点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fauve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; few | peu | shao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;少，很少的，极少的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>linge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; light | ligero [es] | qing &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;轻的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>honve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; heavy | - | zhong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;重的<br> ▹ <b>honveo</b> &nbsp; 重量</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonurjite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;缓，不急的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>urjite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; urgent | urgent | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;急，紧急的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>taute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | tôt | zao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;早的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; late | - | wan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;晚的，迟的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kuaike</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; quick | - | kuai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;快的<br> ▹ <b>kuaikez</b> &nbsp; 加快</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>slane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; slow | lent | man &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;慢的<br> ▹ <b>slanez</b> &nbsp; 拖慢，阻止</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strone</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; strong | foncèe | nong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;浓的（颜色）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; clear | claire | dan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;淡的（颜色）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>douse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; dense | denso [es] | chou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;稠的，浓的（成分比例）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dilite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; dilute | diluèe | xi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;稀的，淡的（成分比例）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>grouse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | grosse | hou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;厚的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mauce</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | mince | bao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;薄的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>denpe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; deep | - | shen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;深的<br> ▹ <b>denpeo</b> &nbsp; 深邃，深沉；深度<br> ▹ <b>denpez</b> &nbsp; 加深，深化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nondenpe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;浅的<br> ▹ <b>nondenpeo</b> &nbsp; 浅薄</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suanfte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; soft | - | ruan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;软的<br> ▹ <b>suanftez</b> &nbsp; 软化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hinde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; hard | - | yin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;硬的<br> ▹ <b>hindez</b> &nbsp; 硬化，加固</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; straight | droite | zhi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;直的，笔直的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kurve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; curved | courbe | qu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;曲的，弯曲的，曲折的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kamre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; square | carré | fang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;方的<br> ▹ <b>kamreo</b> &nbsp; 方形</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rande</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; round | ronde | yuan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;圆的<br> ▹ <b>randeo</b> &nbsp; 圆形，圆饼；小园片，垫圈</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>shanpe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sharp | tranchante | jian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;尖的，尖锐的；锋利的<br> ▹ <b>shanpeo</b> &nbsp; 尖儿<br> ▹ <b>shanpez</b> &nbsp; 削尖；磨锋利</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blunte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; blunt | - | dun &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;钝的，不锋利的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stianke</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sticky | - | nian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;粘的，粘性的，粘乎乎的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>node</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; nude | desnudo [es] | luo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;裸的，裸体的；无装饰的；直率的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>raufe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; rough | raboteuse | cao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;糙的，粗糙的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luase</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | lisse | hua &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;滑的，光滑的，平滑的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sour | - | suan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;酸的<br> ▹ <b>suaneo</b> &nbsp; 酸；醋，醋酸；酸性物质</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dianse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | douxe | tian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;甜的<br> ▹ <b>dianseo</b> &nbsp; 甜；糖</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; bitter | - | ku &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;苦的；涩的；苦涩的，难受的<br> ▹ <b>buteo</b> &nbsp; 苦，苦闷，苦涩</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>spase</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; spicy | épicé | la &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;辣的<br> ▹ <b>spaseo</b> &nbsp; 辣；辣椒</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>friamte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; fragrant | odorant | xiang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;香的<br> ▹ <b>friamteo</b> &nbsp; 香味；香料</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stouke</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; stinky | - | chou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;臭的<br> ▹ <b>stoukeo</b> &nbsp; 臭味</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sianle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; salty | sale | xian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;咸的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nabe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; numb | - | ma &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;麻的；麻木的<br> ▹ <b>nabeo</b> &nbsp; 麻木，麻醉；花椒；麻醉剂</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>frende</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | froide | leng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;冷的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>friamche</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | fraîche | liang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;凉的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vune</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; warm | - | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;温的，温暖的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>heute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; hot | - | re &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;热的<br> ▹ <b>heuteo</b> &nbsp; 热，热量<br> ▹ <b>heutez</b> &nbsp; 热，加热</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>drane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; dry | - | gan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;干的，干燥的<br> ▹ <b>dranez</b> &nbsp; 弄干，使干燥</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mauste</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; moist | mouillée | chao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;湿的，潮湿的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>krende</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; crude | crue | sheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;生的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rupe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; ripe | - | shu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;熟的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>june</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; junior | jeune | shao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;少，年少的，年轻的<br> ▹ <b>juneo</b> &nbsp; 年轻；年轻人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aude</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; old | - | lao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;老，年老的，年长的<br> ▹ <b>audeo</b> &nbsp; 旧的东西；老掉牙的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>famte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; fat | - | pang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;胖的<br> ▹ <b>famteo</b> &nbsp; 胖子</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mougre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; meagre | maigre | shou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;瘦的<br> ▹ <b>mougreo</b> &nbsp; 瘦子</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nine</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; new | nouveau | xin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;新的<br> ▹ <b>nineo</b> &nbsp; 新的东西；新鲜事<br> ▹ <b>ninez</b> &nbsp; 翻新</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vioule</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | vieille | jiu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;旧的，老的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>plane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; plenty | plein | man &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;满的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vakonje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;空的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ronje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; rouge | rouge | hong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;红的<br> ▹ <b>ronjeo</b> &nbsp; 红色，红色的东西<br> ▹ <b>ronjez</b> &nbsp; 染红</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>oranjenje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;橙色的<br> ▹ <b>oranjenjeo</b> &nbsp; 橙色，橙色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>juamne</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; yellow | jaune | huang &gt; 绿色，绿色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; blue | bleue | lan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;蓝的<br> ▹ <b>blaneo</b> &nbsp; 蓝色，蓝色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; violet | violette | zi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;紫的<br> ▹ <b>vileo</b> &nbsp; 紫色，紫色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rense</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; rose | rose | fen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;粉的，玫瑰色的<br> ▹ <b>renseo</b> &nbsp; 粉色，粉色的东西</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>grise</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; grey | grise | hui &gt; 铲平，使...平整</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stoupe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; steep | escarpée | dou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;陡的，陡峭的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>punre</b>&nbsp; #### 品质心态
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>able</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; able | capable | - &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;能的，有能力的<br> ▹ <b>ableo</b> &nbsp; 能力</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>strame</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; strong | - | qiang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;强的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>foble</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; feeble | faible | ruo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;弱的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>facile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; facile | facile | yi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;易，容易的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonfacile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;难，困难的<br> ▹ <b>nonfacileo</b> &nbsp; 困难，困难的事</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>intelije</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; intelligent | intelligent | zhi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;智能的，智慧的；聪明的<br> ▹ <b>intelijeo</b> &nbsp; 智能，智力<br> ▹ <b>intelijez</b> &nbsp; 智能化，使…智能</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vuize</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; wise | - | hui &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;智慧的<br> ▹ <b>vuizeo</b> &nbsp; 智慧；智者</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>smonte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; smart | smart | chong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;聪明的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vuale</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; wily | - | hua &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;滑头的，狡猾的，狡诈的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>stupende</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; stupid | stupide | ben &gt; 贫穷；穷人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ruche</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; rich | riche | fu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;富裕的，富的<br> ▹ <b>rucheo</b> &nbsp; 富裕；富人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bronve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; brave | brave | yong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;勇敢的，大胆的，无畏的<br> ▹ <b>bronveo</b> &nbsp; 勇敢；勇士</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>timode</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;急躁的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>franke</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; frank | franche | tan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;坦诚的，坦白的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>honente</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; honest | honnête | cheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;诚实的<br> ▹ <b>honenteo</b> &nbsp; 诚实</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>hanble</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; humble | humble | qian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;谦虚的，卑谦的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>guilte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; guilty | - | zui &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;有罪的，有犯罪感的；内疚的<br> ▹ <b>guilteo</b> &nbsp; 罪犯</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>munde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; mild | mite [it] | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;温和的（事物）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tunde</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; tender | tendre | wen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;温柔的，温和的（人）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pamle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; pale | pâle | cang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;苍白的，暗淡的；无力的</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
#### 属性类别
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>entenre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; entire | entière | zheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;整体的，全部的<br> ▹ <b>entenreo</b> &nbsp; 全部，整体</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>majure</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; major | majeur | zhu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;主要的，大部分的<br> ▹ <b>majureo</b> &nbsp; 主体，主要部分</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>partule</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; partial | partie | bu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;部分的<br> ▹ <b>partuleo</b> &nbsp; 部分，局部</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>minaure</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; minor | mineur | shao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;少数的<br> ▹ <b>minaureo</b> &nbsp; 少数；少数民族</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sevire</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; several | - | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;几，几个</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pripre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | propre | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;自己的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>privite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; private | privado [es] | si &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;私人的，私有的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>publonke</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; public | publique | gong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;公共的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>certe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; certain | certain | - &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;某个，某</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>evre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; every | - | mei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;每个</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>aute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; other | autre | ta &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;其它的，其余的；另外的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ene</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; any | - | ren &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;任何的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tote</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; total | tout | suo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;所有的，全体的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>some</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; some | - | mou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;一些，某些</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>none</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; none | ne | - &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;没有的，不存在的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>danme</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; half | demie | ban &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;一半的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>etraije</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; foreign | étranger | wai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;外来的，国外的，外国的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>natuve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; native | natif | tu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;土生的，原生的，本地的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>saveje</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; savage | sauvage | ye &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;野生的，野外的；狂野的<br> ▹ <b>savejeo</b> &nbsp; 野蛮；野蛮人</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sule</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sole | seulle | du &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;单独的；孤独的；唯一的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>previanse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; previous | previo [es] | qian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;前面的，之前的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>postoure</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; posterior | postérieure | hou &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;后面的，之后的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>niaste</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; next | - | xia &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;下一次；次于的；紧接的<br> ▹ <b>niasteo</b> &nbsp; 下一个；下一次</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lamste</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; last | - | shang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;上一次；最近的；最后的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>pamste</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; past | passée | wang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;往昔的，往日的，过往的，过去的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>kurante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; current | courant | xian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;现在的，目前的，当前的，当下的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>futuire</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; future | future | wei &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;未来的，将来的，后来的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>maksame</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; maximum | maximale | da &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;最大的<br> ▹ <b>maksameo</b> &nbsp; 最大值</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>miniaume</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; minimum | minimale | xiao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;最小的<br> ▹ <b>miniaumeo</b> &nbsp; 最小值</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>propeure</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; proper | propre | he &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;合适的，恰当的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>finiante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; finite |  | xian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;有限的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonfiniante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;无限的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jenure</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; general | générale | pu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;普遍的，普通的，一般的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prime</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; primary | primaire | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;基本的，主要的，初级的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>necesire</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; necessary | nécessaire | bi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;必要的，必须的，必需的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sianple</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; simple | simple | jian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;简，简单的<br> ▹ <b>sianplez</b> &nbsp; 简化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>komplikante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; complicated | compliqué | fan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;繁，复杂的<br> ▹ <b>komplikantez</b> &nbsp; 复杂化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>speceule</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; special | spéciale | te &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;特别的，特色的；专门的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>distinkte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; distinct | distincte | qing &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;清晰的，明显的，独特的<br> ▹ <b>distinkteo</b> &nbsp; 特点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klinre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; clear | claire | ming &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;明朗的，明白的，清楚的；晴朗的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>blure</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; blurry | brumeuse | hu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;糊的，模糊的（视觉）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vuge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; vague | vague | hu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;糊的，含糊的（语义）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>klinse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; close | - | jin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;近的，临近的（位置）<br> ▹ <b>klinseo</b> &nbsp; 近处；近邻，邻居<br> ▹ <b>klinsez</b> &nbsp; 接近，靠近</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>luane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; - | loin | yuan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;远的，远离的（位置<br> ▹ <b>luaneo</b> &nbsp; 远处，远方<br> ▹ <b>luanez</b> &nbsp; 远离，离开</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>recinte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; recent | récent(e) | jin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;近期的，最近的（时间）</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>konme</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; common | commune | gong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;共同的，常见的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sonme</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; same | - | tong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;同样的，相同的<br> ▹ <b>sonmeo</b> &nbsp; 相同点，共同点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>simile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; similar | semblable | si &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;相似的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonsonme</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;不同的<br> ▹ <b>nonsonmeo</b> &nbsp; 不同点</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>opanze</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;相反的</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
#### 一般描述
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; right | - | dui &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;对的，正确的<br> ▹ <b>riteo</b> &nbsp; 正确；正确的事；正义<br> ▹ <b>ritez</b> &nbsp; 纠正，改正</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>roge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; wrong | - | cuo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;错的，错误的<br> ▹ <b>rogeo</b> &nbsp; 错误；错误的事<br> ▹ <b>rogez</b> &nbsp; 使…犯错；妨碍</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>trene</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; true | vraie | zhen &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;真的<br> ▹ <b>treneo</b> &nbsp; 真事，真相；真品</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fiase</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; false | faux | jia &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;假的，错的；假冒的<br> ▹ <b>fiaseo</b> &nbsp; 假象；假货，赝品；谎言<br> ▹ <b>fiasez</b> &nbsp; 作假；撒谎</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suide</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; pseudo | pseudo | jia &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;伪的，假性的，伪装的，虚构的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>makoze</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;人造的，人为的；矫揉造作的；假的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>libre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; liberal | libre | zi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;自由的<br> ▹ <b>libreo</b> &nbsp; 自由<br> ▹ <b>librez</b> &nbsp; 使...自由，释放</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>saupe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; super | super | chao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;超级的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>precinse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; precise | précise | jing &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;精确的，准确的<br> ▹ <b>precinseo</b> &nbsp; 精确；精度</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonprecinse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;大约的，大概的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>absuete</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; absent | absente | que &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;缺席的，缺失的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>intankte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; intact | intacte | wan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;完好的，完整的，未受损的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>komplete</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; complete | complète | che &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;彻底的，完全的，完整的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>danjanre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; dangerous | dangereuse | xian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;危险的，险恶的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>danke</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; dark | - | an &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;暗的，灰暗的，黑暗的<br> ▹ <b>dankeo</b> &nbsp; 黑暗；暗淡</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>delicote</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; delicate | délicate | ruo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;脆弱的；纤弱的；纤细的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dirikte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; direct | directe | zhi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;直接的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>extrime</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; extreme | extrême | ji &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;极端的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>furte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; fertile | féconde | fu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;富饶的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mingre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; meagre | maigre | pin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;贫瘠的，贫乏的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>faume</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; firm | ferme | lao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;牢固的，坚定的，结实的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>impaute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; important | importante | yao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;重要的，紧要的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonimpaute</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;不重要的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>posenble</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; possible | possible | neng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;可能的<br> ▹ <b>posenbleo</b> &nbsp; 可能性</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonposenble</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;不可能的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>konveniante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; convenient | commode | bian &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;方便的，合适的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonkonveniante</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; = &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;不便的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>jonste</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; just | juste | gong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;公平的，公正的<br> ▹ <b>jonsteo</b> &nbsp; 公平；正义</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mune</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; mean | moyenne | jun &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;均匀的；平均的<br> ▹ <b>muneo</b> &nbsp; 平均值<br> ▹ <b>munez</b> &nbsp; 平均化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>parinle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; parallel | parallèle | ping &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;平行的<br> ▹ <b>parinleo</b> &nbsp; 平行线</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prezaite</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; present | présente | zai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;在场的，出席的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>perfankte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; perfect | parfaite | wan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;完美的，完整的，完全的；绝对的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>idile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; ideal | idéal | li &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;理想的，完美的；不切实际的<br> ▹ <b>idileo</b> &nbsp; 理想<br> ▹ <b>idilez</b> &nbsp; 理想化</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>praude</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; proud | - | ao &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;骄傲的，傲慢的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rire</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; rare | rare | xi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;稀少的，稀罕的，稀有的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rile</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; real | réelle | shi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;实际的，真实的<br> ▹ <b>rileo</b> &nbsp; 事实，实际情况</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>regamle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; regular | régulière | chang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;常规的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sanfe</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; safe | sauve | an &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;安全的<br> ▹ <b>sanfeo</b> &nbsp; 安全</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sikre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; secret | secrète | mi &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;秘密的，机密的<br> ▹ <b>sikreo</b> &nbsp; 秘密</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sensinte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sensitive | sensible | min &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;敏感的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sevonre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; severe | sévère | zhong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;严<u>重</u>的，严峻的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>seruse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; serious | sérieuse | su &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;严<u>肃</u>的，认真的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>gruve</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; grave | grave | su &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;严<u>肃</u>的，肃穆的，庄重的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>silote</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; silent | silencieuse | mo &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;沉默的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sincenre</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sincere | sincère | cheng &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;诚恳的，诚挚的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sude</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sudden | soudain(e) | tu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;突然的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sufuce</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sufficient | suffisant(e) | zu &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;充足的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>suere</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; sure | sûre | que &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;确定的，确信的；当然</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>teronble</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; terrible | terrible | kong &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;恐怖的，可怕的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lonse</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; loose | lâche | song &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;松的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tinte</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; tight | - | jin &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;紧的，紧身的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>straije</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; strange | strano [it] | guai &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;奇<u>怪</u>的<br> ▹ <b>straijeo</b> &nbsp; 怪事</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>usuamle</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; usual | usuelle | chang &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;通<u>常</u>的，平常的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>ordane</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; ordinary | ordinaire | fan &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;平<u>凡</u>的，普通的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>violiete</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; violent | violente | lie &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;剧<u>烈</u>的，强烈的，粗暴的</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vulge</b>&nbsp; <i><small> &lt; vulgar | vulgaire | su &gt; </small></i>&nbsp;&nbsp;粗<u>俗</u>的，通俗的</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
## 复合词
#### 高频日常
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>bonevenaiz</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;欢迎</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>rekanz</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;再见</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nondankiez</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;不用谢</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nonkua</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;没啥，不用谢</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tautemilan</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;早餐，早饭</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mimilan</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;中餐，中饭</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>lantemilan</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;晚餐，晚饭</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>futubou</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;足球</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>baskanbou</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;篮球</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nuambou</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;网球</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>notibuku</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;笔记本</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>vordibuku</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;词典，字典</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>mikunzebuku</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;杂志</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nuvenpapi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;报纸</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
#### 数字相关
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>unme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第一</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dume</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第二</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>trime</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第三</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fuame</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第四</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cinkme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第五</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sisme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第六</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sepme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第七</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>okme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第八</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>nofme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第九</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dekme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第十</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dekunme</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第十一</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dekdume</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;第十二</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>unrin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;一星，水星</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>durin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;二星，金星</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tririn</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;三星，地球</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fuarin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;四星，火星</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cinkrin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;五星，木星</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sisrin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;六星，土星</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>seprin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;七星，天王星</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>okrin</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;八星，海王星</p><p>&nbsp;</p>
#### 时间相关
<p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prevprevdi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;前天；[副] 在前天</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prevdi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;昨天；[副] 在昨天</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tudi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;今天；[副] 在今天</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>postdi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;明天；[副] 在明天</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>postpostdi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;后天；[副] 在后天</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>prevdinie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;昨晚；[副] 在昨晚</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tudinie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;今晚；[副] 在今晚</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>postdinie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;明晚；[副] 在明晚</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>niedi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;佛晓，黎明</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>premidi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;上午，早上</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>midi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;中午</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>posmidi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;下午</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dinie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;黄昏，傍晚</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>preminie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;晚上，上半夜</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>minie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;午夜，半夜</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>posminie</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;凌晨，下半夜</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>undi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周一</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dudi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周二</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tridi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周三</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fuadi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周四</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cinkdi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周五</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sisdi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周六</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>solidi</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;周日</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>untue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;一月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>dutue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;二月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>tritue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;三月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>fuatue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;四月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>cinktue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;五月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>sistue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;六月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>septue</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;七月</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em 0em"><b>borenzo-dian</b>&nbsp;&nbsp;生日</p><p style="text-indent:-3em;padding:3em;margin:-3em 0em -5em
